R: Jane was a professor teaching piano to students.
S: Jane spent the morning sipping coffee and reading a book.
X: Two of Jane's students were early for their lessons.
Y: None of Jane's students had a lesson that day.
A: Let's think step by step.First, we need to identify which sentence describes observation R and which describes observation S. Observation R is about Jane teaching piano to students, so X describes R. Observation S is about Jane sipping coffee and reading a book, so Y describes S. 

Now, we need to determine which sentence describes the observations more plausibly. X describes two of Jane's students being early for their lessons, which is a plausible observation if Jane is a piano teacher. Y describes none of Jane's students having a lesson that day, which is not a plausible observation if Jane is a piano teacher. 

Therefore, the sentence that describes the observations more plausibly is X. The answer is X.
